***moe.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moe.html>moe</a> (870)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moede.html>moede</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loss.html>loss</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i>-d-</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:moede.html>moede</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:tired.html>tired</a>, loath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">muothi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:tired.html>tired</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*mōþaz</i>.

***moederlijk.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:moederlijk.html>moederlijk</a> (43397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-lijk</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moederlijk.html>moederlijk</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:moederlijk.html>moederlijker</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">moederlijkst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>maternal</li></ol>
